SELECT up_id, dbo.fGetNearestObjIdEq(up_ra,up_dec,#) as objId   FROM #upload WHERE dbo.fGetNearestObjIdEq(up_ra,up_dec,#) IS NOT NULL  EXEC spExecuteSQL '  SELECT u.up_Name as [Name], x.objID, e.specObjID, e.ra, e.dec, e.Flux_OII_#, e.Flux_OII_#_Err, e.AoN_OII_#, e.Fit_Warning_OII_#, e.Flux_OII_#, e.Flux_OII_#_Err, e.AoN_OII_#, e.Fit_Warning_OII_#, e.Flux_Ha_#, e.Flux_Ha_#_Err, e.AoN_Ha_#, e.Fit_Warning_Ha_#,e.Flux_Hb_#, e.Flux_Hb_#_Err, e.AoN_Hb_#, e.Fit_Warning_Hb_#, e.Flux_OIII_#, e.Flux_OIII_#_Err, e.AoN_OIII_#, e.Fit_Warning_OIII_#, e.Flux_OI_#, e.Flux_OI_#_Err, e.AoN_OI_#, e.Fit_Warning_OI_#, e.Flux_NII_#, e.Flux_NII_#_Err, e.AoN_NII_#, e.Fit_Warning_NII_#, e.Flux_SII_#, e.Flux_SII_#_Err, e.AoN_SII_#, e.Fit_Warning_SII_#, s.snMedian, s.zWarning, s.z FROM #upload u  JOIN #x x ON x.up_id = u.up_id  JOIN emissionLinesPort e ON e.specObjID = x.specObjID  JOIN SpecObjAll s ON s.specObjID = x.specObjID WHERE  s.zWarning=# AND  s.snMedian > # AND  s.class=GALAXY
